Free Talk

The Essayification of the Novel 229

— Mu Mutian

There is a noteworthy phenomenon in the current Chinese literary scene: the essayification of the novel. This seems connected to the recent flourishing of humorous sketches and "essays of the mind." It is also related to the current social environment in China. The emptiness of life leads people to gravitate towards "easy literature" (la Littérature Facile).

Essay-style novels are much easier to write than serious novels. Choosing the easy path of writing essay-style novels reveals the writer's lack of a serious creative attitude and an unfulfilled life.

A friend who edits a magazine told me, "Lately, some works are simply indistinguishable between novels and essays." This trend is visibly growing day by day, becoming more and more prominent.

I believe that novels and essays are different genres in literature, with strict distinctions between them.

Novel scholars like Hamilton say that novels must have elements such as structure, characters, and setting. England, as the advanced country of modern industrial capitalism, developed the novel form earliest. Lyly, Richardson, Fielding, and others set many requirements for the novel. Therefore, anything that contradicts the conditions of the novel—lacking structure, characters, and setting—can be called an essay or prose.

In terms of its social foundation, the novel is a product of the upwardly mobile bourgeoisie, while essays are products of the aristocracy or literati. Novels have structure, plot twists, and story development, while essays are leisurely and rambling, often close to poetry and a prose substitute for poetry.

Of course, this refers to novels before the last century. By the late 19th century, in the atmosphere of aestheticism, impressionism, and symbolism—a reaction against realism—most writers abandoned reality, daring not to face la bêtise humaine. Some novels abandoned the task of social representation, and the trend of essayification of the novel grew daily. A significant example of this is much of Anatole France's work.

Generally speaking, the essayification of the novel is not an upward trend. It contains a kind of crisis. The giant André Gide, a man with the strongest artistic conscience and the fiercest pursuit of desire, only acknowledges "The Counterfeiters" as a proper novel (roman) among his many works. His insightful and far-sightedness is imaginable. When essays invade the realm of the novel, should our writers strive for a "defense of the novel"? Should we protect the independence of the novel form?

I believe that we must pay special attention to this trend of essayification of the novel. We must constantly prevent the development of "easy literature." On one hand, our writers must create new and more advanced novel forms, and on the other hand, they must constantly defend against the crisis of the essayification of the novel.

West Lake Daily Record (5) 230

— Yu Dafu

(Traveling to West Tianmu)

March 30th, Friday, cloudy and sunny. West Tianmu Mountain belongs to Qian County. Yesterday, I got off the train at a small station named Zaoxi. From there I took a sedan chair north for thirty or forty li. Midway, I passed Jiaokou Ridge, which was about one or two hundred zhang high. After passing Jiaokou Ridge, the scenery on all sides changed. Outside the ridge was a world of small mountains and barren fields, desolate and unbearable. Inside the ridge to the north, the lofty Tianmu was right in front of me. Clear streams flowed beside the road; naturally, these were the Shuangqing streams flowing down from the southern foot of Tianmu Mountain. Sometimes converging, sometimes separating, the streams sometimes met the road. There were many villages, the fields were fertile, and there were many bridges and roadside pavilions, to say nothing of other things. After passing the Baihe Bridge over the Baihe Stream and the Moon Bridge, the road ascended gradually. After entering Dayou Village, I was already on the mountain road. The sky was overcast, the trees were dark and dense. As soon as I reached the mountain gate, in this dark net where the night and tree shadows competed, I soon heard the hypnotic suggestion of bells, drums, and chanting. A feeling of prolonged fear,寂滅, conversion, and world-renunciation suddenly struck my mind like lightning. The mysterious power of religion and the possibility of miracles were fully comprehended here. This was partly due to the lateness of the hour, and partly, I think, because I was tired from a day of travel, and my muscles and energy were a little relaxed.

The founder of West Tianmu was the Chan master Gao Feng from Wujiang, born in the Jiaxi era of the Yuan dynasty. His place of practice was the Lion Rock Head of West Peak. To this day, there is still a place called the "Dead Pass," which was the name Gao Feng Chan Master used when he was practicing. The Chan Master's bone pagoda is now in the Lion Mouth below Lion Peak. From the Yuan to the Ming dynasties, the temples and monasteries of West Tianmu were all built around the Lion Peak, the so-called Lion Orthodox Chan Temple. Before the Yuan dynasty, the name of West Tianmu Mountain was not clearly seen in the classics. Su Dongpo did not visit it during his county travels, nor did Xie An leave any traces of his mountain excursions there. During the Yuan and Ming dynasties, the temple was repeatedly abandoned and rebuilt. It was not until the Kangxi era of the Qing dynasty that the National Teacher Yulin began to build the Gao Feng Daocheng at the base of the current Chanyuan Temple, which was actually a variant of the Qingzhuang ruins built by Yuan Hongqiao's ancestor who donated fields. In the gloomy night, the sedan chair arrived at the mountain gate. Getting out of the sedan chair, I saw a huge eight-character yellow wall, with wooden frames scattered inside and outside. It seemed that the mountain gate of this sacred mountain of Tianmu was under construction. After entering the gate and walking for one or two li, the ground rose a section. Entering the Hall of the Heavenly Kings. After another section higher, entering the Hall of Weituo Bodhisattva. Again a section higher, there was a plaque with the words "Xingdao" hanging there, the Dharma Hall. From here, section after section, higher and higher, passing the Grand Hall of the Great Hero, passing through the abbot's residence, winding and circling, it took over ten minutes to reach the guest room on the eastern five-bay upstairs hall. The windows were bright, the tables were clean, the lamps were bright, and the room was deep. The furnishings were like those of a top-notch hotel in Shanghai, only missing a few electric lights and a few female believers selling songs and bodies.

It was the evening of the 15th day of the second lunar month. After a very comfortable vegetarian dinner, the clouds broke and the moon came out. From the corridor, I could see many green peaks and black shadows in front of and behind the temple, as well as a winding mountain stream full of strange rocks. The sound of the stream was sonorous, and the moonlight was blurred. Yu Tang, who had just finished reading the twenty-eighth chapter of "A Rustic's Exposure," was on the corridor with a cigar in his mouth, looking into the distance with his hands behind his back. Returning to the hearth, he exclaimed: "This is truly an excellent Dichtung!" Unfortunately, the mountainside was full of snow, and the outside air was sharp and cold. Facing this clear and empty night, we could only reluctantly give it up. After eating some peanuts bought from the vendors in the Hall of the Heavenly Kings and drinking some local wine with a peculiar taste, the few Dichters had no choice but to go to bed with resentment and dream their own dreams.

At seven in the morning, the poets' dreams were broken by the clear singing of mountain birds. Everyone got up to wash and have breakfast, and then prepared to take sedan chairs up the mountain to see the sights. Yu Tang caught a bit of a cold and was unwilling to move, only wanting to lie on the monk's bed in Chanyuan Temple and read "A Rustic's Exposure," so he did not go.

To—— 231

— Hei Ying

From the day I first saw you, there was a devout hope, silently, silently—

I placed it on you.

Because you have strong arms; because your strength is

the kind that has built iron bridges and skyscrapers.

When you are tired and resting,

sleeping in bed to restore your energy,

do you think about your even greater work waiting to begin?

You who have built iron bridges and skyscrapers,

you warrior of this era!

I hold a devout hope for you;

Many important tasks await your—shoulder!

Chinese Mastery 232

— Yi Ren

It was one day in the deep autumn of 1928. I suffered a severe bout of malaria in Hangzhou and had to return to Wuhan in disappointment. When passing through Shanghai, because a friend who promised to lend me twenty dollars temporarily broke his promise, I had to travel in steerage.

At dusk, a bleak drizzle fell. The only friend who saw me off was Gu Cheng. Because there would be fewer squabbles with ticket-scalping soldiers and other disturbances on a foreign ship, I boarded a ship of the XX Company. Luckily, there was one upper berth left in steerage, so I booked it. As I was making the bed, Gu Cheng bought a large bunch of bananas from the shore. The passengers in the lower berth were a young girl and a woman in her forties. Hearing our Hunan accent, they began to claim the same home with us in a Hubei accent—saying that Hunan and Hubei were one family. Fearing that I would be too lonely on the ship, Gu Cheng was happy to chat with them for a while. We talked and ate bananas for a while, and then Gu Cheng said goodbye and went ashore... I stood at the ship's door, watching Gu Cheng's black shadow disappear in the misty rain, and I felt very lost in my heart. I returned to the cabin and soon fell asleep.

When I woke up, the ship had entered the Yangtze River quite far. Although it was not long after dawn, I was already a little hungry. After washing my face and drinking milk, I still felt bored, so I went to the side of the ship to see the scenery. There was nothing much to see. However, when I returned to the cabin, I found something that piqued my curiosity... The two Hubei women sleeping in the lower berth had unfolded a large part of my mattress and hung it from the edge of the bed—as if it were a curtain; what was covered inside was the two women lying horizontally smoking opium. There was nothing unusual about smoking opium, but their technique of making the bubbles, the dexterity of their hands, did make me admire them and feel a sense of appreciation... The girl held a copper coin in her left hand and a shiny iron needle in her right hand. She used the shiny iron needle to pick a bit of opium paste from a small opium box—just the right amount—and then, very deftly, she burned it on the lamp while rotating it on the copper coin. She was able to prevent it from burning and rotate it without it sticking to the copper coin... Her technique had already impressed me very much. Then I saw that the woman's technique was even better... When she burned it on the lamp, it was just about to burn and stop, about to drip and not drop. When she rotated it on the copper coin, one turn was perfectly round, manipulating it freely, nothing was not just right. After they had enough of their addiction, they extinguished the lamp and apologized to me, putting my mattress back in place. But I was still very interested and felt that my appreciation was not enough. So I went elsewhere to look for opium smokers to watch. (To be continued)

Views on Love from Famous People Around the World 233

— Ma Zongrong

10. Marriage comes from love, and vinegar comes from wine; it is a measured drink, not very palatable and bitter. Time makes it lose its heavenly fragrance and turns it into a household, tasteless, and ordinary drink. (Byron - English)

11. Women, never trust the vows of men... In order to get what they fervently desire, they are less sparing of vows than they are of promises; as soon as their desires are satisfied, they immediately forget their promises and their vows. (Catullus - Latin poet)

12. Lovers who do not quarrel are about to stop loving each other. (Ovid - Latin poet)

13. If you hear a woman slandering love, and a man of letters expressing dissatisfaction with public opinion, you can say that one has lost her beauty, and the other has exhausted his talent. (Diderot - French)

14. Women love, but do not know how to use love. (Alexandre Dumas fils - French)

15. Do not boast that the woman you love very much loves you very much. (Pythagoras - Greek)

16. What is generally called love in the world is not love; it is extreme selfishness... it is loving oneself in another person. (Esquiros - French)

17. No passion is more likely to arouse some noble or brave heart in us than sincere love. Love has a kind of heat that can give courage to those who lack courage. (Saint-Évremond - French)

18. The arguments of lovers are precisely what renew their love. (Terence - Latin poet)

19. The most disgraced mistress, as soon as she shows that she loves another man more than her lover, can make him restless and arouse all sorts of passionate shadows in his heart. (Stendhal - French)

Travel Musings 234

— Liu Ming

Walking in the wilderness, sometimes you need a bit of muddled ignorance; if you are too often sensitive, it will only cause more pain. This is not just a whim, but the experience I gained from my previous travels in the Gaoligong Mountains.

I remember that the mountain road that day followed a winding mountain stream. Trees grew profusely along the sides of the stream. Looking up, it was difficult to catch a glimpse of the sky and clouds. All along the way, I only saw the rushing stream, often bursting out from the winding thickets, colliding with jagged rocks, splashing pearls, laughing and jumping like a child, rushing down the slope past me. Sometimes, the mountain road would wind to the other side of the stream, and I had to step on the protruding stones in the water to cross. Sometimes, even this would happen... Suddenly, the mountain road and the stream seemed to disappear completely, and all that stood before me were towering cliffs and dense forests. However, once I climbed past the small path on the cliff, in the blink of an eye, the previous scenery would all reappear. I think that even if you walked all day on such a journey, no one would feel any fatigue, right?

When I was almost finished walking this mountain road, I suddenly encountered someone coming from the opposite direction, carrying a long knife in his hand, which immediately frightened me. The whistling I had been doing along the way immediately stopped, and I quietly held my breath. But he walked past me with a look of panic, glancing at me and hurrying past. I took a deep breath and looked closely at the small bamboo basket tied on his back. It was filled with potatoes and fruits. Only then did I realize that he was not a "bandit grandpa," but just a passing farmer, carrying a knife only to protect himself. It was then that I realized that this mountain road was probably not very safe. However, it could also be said that perhaps that person was too nervous? In short, from the beginning, I had not been sensitive to "meeting a bandit grandpa," but had simply moved forward in a muddled state. In any case, this could be considered fortunate. Even if someone suddenly ended my life with a knife along the way, it would be more comfortable and enjoyable than being frightened all the way and then meeting misfortune.

Therefore, if you want to move forward frankly on the journey of life and suffer less pain, then I think you should also be like walking in the wilderness, sometimes you must have a bit of muddled ignorance.

A Woman (5) 235

— Wang Yue

"It's true, 'home is good for a thousand days,' alas..." After a moment of silence, he lowered his head and sighed, then leaned against the wall with his buttocks, swung his arms twice, and began to tell, in a confused and mixed way, about his hardships as a wanderer and his wife and children, whom he had left in a small house in his hometown, and now there was no news of them. His narration was interrupted from time to time by hiccups caused by alcohol, and he repeatedly asked:

"What do you say?"

"Um, um..." After being asked many times, she reluctantly responded, shrinking and retreating into the alley. "Oh, a mute?" the man asked in surprise, and then he exclaimed in the tone of thinking it over in his mind, "Really a mute?"

"Um..." She had already disappeared into the shadows, but the man still stood there, one eye staring at the street lamp, his hand scratching the beard on his protruding chin. In a moment of contemplation, he sighed with a feeling of being tormented by loneliness: "There's really no way..." Then he followed her to the place where she had disappeared, and only left that human nest the next morning, rubbing his eyes. But after that, he would visit from time to time, for a little cold rice or pocket money, until the widow discovered their secret. This burly woman, with her hands stuck in the pockets of her wool vest, like a hen that had just laid an egg, laughed and ran through every kitchen, and in front of the assembled crowd she put forward her clever guess:

"What if she hooks up with a thief?"

"Oh, no wonder I lost two washcloths the other day!" A woman with a freckled face exclaimed, stirring her pot. Then everyone became nervous, and a proposal for expulsion was immediately passed in the feelings of disgust and worry of the owners. So on this morning, she had to pack up all her property (which was so meager that it was like a bit of irony to our laws... because she only had a broken bowl and some cotton wool like a fishing net), leave this alley, walking in her solitary way through the alley, amidst the ridicule of the people, under the impartial sunshine... (The End)

Difficulties in the Development of the Banking Industry 238

This year, various industries have been affected by the trends of the times. Not only are they in a state of decline, but also the situation in various aspects is silent and stagnant. For example, the current silk cocoon and tea industries, which in previous years would have been thriving, are now facing a bleak future. According to recent investigations, people in the industry are afraid to engage in long-term business. The market atmosphere is declining, and the banking industry is only receiving and not lending. If this continues, there may be unimaginable consequences. It is observed that although the interbank lending rate in the morning and afternoon markets yesterday was slightly better at 2 fen, calculated at 5 fen, it is ultimately not a good sign due to the lack of smooth circulation. Random Thoughts

Beauty Trap 253

— Ya Fei

Japan's diplomatic tactics can truly be described as "constantly innovating" and "nothing is too strange." First, they use the facade of friendship to deceive the world, fabricating stories out of thin air to confuse public opinion. Then, they resort to vile actions to lobby various countries, showering them with sweet words and flattery to the best of their ability. Further on, they expose their ferocious nature and implement decisive measures. Nothing could be more despicable and contemptible!

Recently, those directors of world dramas are again stirring up trouble, adding fuel to the fire to expand the stage for their performance. Whether it's a comedy or a tragedy, we should watch closely. Ultimately, they are wielding both carrot and stick, employing their clever and treacherous political and diplomatic tactics. Taking advantage of the military and political turmoil in various countries, they are simultaneously plotting the permanent annexation of the entire North China region and striving to ease tensions with Soviet Russia and attempting to connect with the United States, while also sabotaging US-Russian reconciliation. However, this plan ultimately failed, and their underhanded schemes were unable to proceed, leaving them with nothing but futile sighs. Yet, who knows if they will change their strategies to realize their dreams?

Previously, Japan's instigation of African independence was also one of their subtle and cunning diplomatic maneuvers, but it too soon ended in failure. However, they are determined to uphold the motto that "failure is the mother of success." Therefore, even though they have repeatedly failed, they are not discouraged. They continue their efforts, determined to satisfy their ambitions. As such, they have recently launched a full-scale diplomatic campaign, lobbying, co-opting, sabotaging, and engaging in activities in every corner of the world and without regard to any detail. Their numerous schemes and ugly behavior are both pitiful and hateful! In April, newspapers reported: "A dispatch from the China United News Agency on the 2nd stated that the Abyssinian royal family in the black African country wants to marry a Japanese woman as a candidate for Empress. Ms. Masako Kuroda, the second daughter of Viscount Kuroda, has been chosen. This policy is similar to Kawashima Yoshiko's marriage to the Mongolian prince, albeit with different methods. The Japanese military and political circles have high expectations for this. However, due to numerous obstacles, the 'beauty trap' failed. Japan claims that Italy secretly prevented this from happening, and the Abyssinian Foreign Minister had no choice but to cancel the engagement." From this, it is clear that the Japanese's conspiracies and schemes are obvious everywhere, and there is no need for further elaboration. However, I recall that Kawashima Yoshiko's offering to the Mongolian prince was also a similar tactic. Who knew that this time, Italy would obstruct the plan, causing their "beauty trap" to fail? One can imagine how bitterly they resent Italy.

Recently, it was reported that Japan shipped a large number of plants to the United States, secretly containing a large amount of potent toxins. However, the US authorities discovered this and detained the shipment, preventing their plot from succeeding. However, their sinister and cruel intentions are evident from this incident.

After the puppet of the Northeast, Pu Yi, ascended the throne in the so-called "Manchukuo," the Japanese immediately offered him several beautiful Japanese women for entertainment, to alleviate his loneliness. Their affection is truly considerate in every detail. However, what is their true intention? Is it goodwill, or is there another purpose? It is not difficult for us to discern their underlying motives. They are using the lure of beauty and pleasure to monitor Pu Yi's actions, preventing him from stepping out of line. The depth of their scheming and the meticulousness of their planning are beyond the comprehension of our ignorant countrymen! Alas!

Miss Cherry Blossom 254

— Bei Bei

One early morning, the golden sunlight, gently, shone on the two floor-to-ceiling windows with their thin square grilles at the front of a bedroom! The thin wire mesh, plated with nickel, allowed one to vaguely make out the tiny squares through the inner silk gauze curtains, like a pattern painted by a great artist!

Outside was a small courtyard, planted with many red and yellow wintersweet flowers! The ripe fragrance was released, filling the quietness. From the gridded long windows, passing through the extremely thin silk gauze, the whole room was filled with that fragrance!

Next to the window was a newly purchased "Simmons" spring sofa. At this moment, it was crowded with piles of candy and the discarded wrappers. There was also a pair of pure goatskin gloves, with slender fingers! One could guess that they would not fit just any man.

A small mirror inlaid with a large square was also present!

In the eastern corner was a small triangular dresser, covered with a patterned tablecloth. On top of it was a large "RCA" radio, its power cord snaked out, with the plug inserted but not removed!

Next to it was a pair of small "armchairs," close to the bed.

The bed was open and disheveled, almost in the middle of the entire room!

The circular canopy, hung down from the very center, and was tied at the bottom with a red silk knot!

Warm spring has arrived! It is melancholy! Because its mistress is out of sorts.

The mistress, the intelligent mistress丨Miss Cherry Blossom! Was wrapped up in a milky white quilt.

The little angels' bell had just rung six times. It was still so early!

Little Plum also hadn't gotten up yet. Sleeping in the back, in the small iron

Page 18

If they can’t bring themselves to die, they enact a suicide scene. They (or she) see suicide as the only escape, the only way to resolve all their issues.

In the past month, several tragic suicide cases have occurred on campus…

One rainy evening, the resident advisor was taking roll call. Miss × was missing from her dormitory. Her suicide note was discovered in the disciplinary office the next evening. It read roughly as follows:

“...Being alive, I cannot find the joy of life, only its bitterness. Therefore, I shall throw myself into the vast and boundless sea, following the surging waves. Ah! The world is a grand stage, and everyone plays a role. I have acted in a tragedy, so I will be the first to leave the stage. Life, love, money, these remain unsolvable mysteries. Ah! Mysteries, the taste of love I have already tried, and tried several times, but I have failed. Their flavors are bitter and spicy... Farewell, my teachers, my friends...”

From this, we know that she went to commit suicide, and we infer that she must have thrown herself into the sea or the Huangpu River. Therefore, the students at school had a new topic of conversation. Several students, known for their nosiness like detectives, told me the following:

"Miss × gave the gatekeeper three yuan, so the gatekeeper let her leave without permission..."

Hearing about the gatekeeper taking money on the sly, an inexplicable sense of revulsion rose in my heart, so I interrupted the student and exclaimed loudly, "What's the big deal about the gatekeeper taking money on the sly? Didn't Miss × tell me personally that she paid the gatekeeper two yuan for the convenience of leaving? And didn't ×× give him six dimes to go see a movie? There are so many things like this!"

"That's right! The school staff only think about 'getting a cut,' taking money on the sly and slacking off. The school only cares about collecting tuition and ignores everything else. Students make dates to see movies and engage in romance, putting their studies behind them. Ah! This is the life of professors, students, and staff in a university! But now I will tell you more about Miss ×'s affair! It is said that Miss × had been in love with three men, but she abandoned them due to her insatiable vanity, causing herself suffering and ending up in this state."

Miss ×'s tragedy clearly exposes the internal contradictions of the youth of this era. Ah! Contradictions, people live in such contradictions.

Novel

Between Flesh and Blood (5) 257

— Man Zhi

(II)

Sixth Master returned home and went straight to his wife's room, but she wasn't there. He turned around and went to the small dining room in the back, where his wife and daughter-in-law were waiting for dinner. Sixth Master didn't say a word, just ate his food, his face no different than usual. The daughter-in-law stood beside him serving him, naturally not daring to say a word. Sixth Master's wife had originally wanted to speak but didn't dare given the situation. The servants, such as the maids, the old nannies, and the old servant Pu Ning, didn't even dare to cough. It was raining softly outside the eaves.

Sixth Master suddenly stopped eating, looked at his wife, and said,

"That beast is back. I don't want to see him. Don't call him to see me! It's not right for him to live in the house. If he has nowhere to go, the new house in the back is empty, tell him to live there." He glanced at Pu Ning and said, "Pu Ning is enough to accompany him!" After eating a few bites, he said, "A karmic debt from a previous life, to give birth to this child who harms his parents!"

His wife replied, "It's truly a karmic debt! He doesn't dare to see you either, no need to be angry. This kind of child who harms his parents only causes me grief and doesn't give me any blessings. I don't want to see him either!"

The daughter-in-law felt saddened that she had married such a husband who didn't earn money or gain fame to honor his parents, instead causing his parents to hate him. Her nose twitched, and tears welled up in her eyes.

After dinner, Sixth Master went to his wife's room to wash his face and instructed the maid drawing water to ask his wife to come. Sixth Master picked up his wife's water pipe and smoked, and when his wife entered the room, she asked what was the matter. Sixth Master didn't immediately speak, and his wife, thinking he was angry, didn't dare to ask further and went to wash her face. After she washed her face, she sat on a chair, watching Sixth Master pacing back and forth in the room.

Sixth Master suddenly stopped, and said indignantly,

"Do you still want this son?"

"Do you still want this son?"

His wife became somewhat saddened, her voice nearly choked with tears,

"I've already lost hope in him! Raising him for over twenty years, not a single day has passed without causing me grief. He was sick when he was a child, and now he's causing trouble outside! Even though he's back now, the officials still want to arrest him, and the family will lose money again! A child who harms his parents, how can I hope he'll support me in my old age?... But my second son, Jianming, is still young, and I don't know how he'll turn out in the future. Why is my life so bitter!" As she spoke, tears streamed down her face!

Sixth Master said, "Jianming seems to be following the rules and studying hard in Shantou. Of course, I hope for more good sons, but one bad son is already too much! Now!" He raised his head and saw the maid standing by the door, shouting, "Get out!" The maid was startled and ran to the kitchen. "Now that this beast is back, whether we want him or not is in our hands! I've already discussed it with Second Master, we'll kill him ourselves!"

Movie Special

The Atmosphere and Local Color of Film 258

— Lan Wu

I remember a film that seemed to be called "Scandals of England" (?) opened with an extremely dense morning fog, people moving in the haze*.

The fog is a characteristic of London, indicating that the film is set in London. But what followed was old-fashioned carriages on the streets of London*,

This, in addition to illustrating London, further illustrates the conservative nature of the British. In the fog, only a very small number*

Of pedestrians and cars were present, only the sound of a milk cart bell heard slowly approaching from afar, then slowly fading away. This allowed the audience to become drunk*

Enchanted in the poetic atmosphere of morning fog in the streets. As for using war as a background, it is of course possible to depict a war atmosphere filled with ominous sounds and panic*.

It is not necessary for a real war to appear. Even in war films, the terrifying atmosphere of war does not lie in the earth-shattering cannon fire*,

And the sound of machine guns like a string of pearls, but rather in the mournful whinnying of wounded horses during or after the war.

If Chinese films want to create a peaceful atmosphere of rural life, they often use willow ponds and the sounds of geese, which is of course possible. But I feel that if*

They can film a distant view of a vast plain with ripe grain filling the fields, followed by a close-up of an ox cart fully loaded returning*; Special attention should be paid to the brilliant rays of the setting sun, shining on*

The side of the ox cart filled with grain. Followed by a close-up of the head of the farmer driving the ox cart; The sunlight paints*

A smile on the straw hat. Following that, a distant view of a small village with wisps of smoke rising from the chimneys, on a road, the ox cart gradually walks further and further, eventually*

"Fading out." If it is a sound film, then in the first long shot, the sound of field songs gradually comes closer, in the second close-up the singing is a little louder,*

In the third close-up, singing. In the fourth long shot, the singing gradually fades away again. This is not "a purely aesthetic appreciation of the free world without purpose"*

But rather "mixing the natural world with the people around it" (G. Nela Tofu's preface to "The Iron Flood"). This is more powerful than willow ponds and the sounds of geese by*

I don't know how much? If we want to strengthen the effect of the film, the atmosphere of the film is worth noting.

Similar to atmosphere but actually different is what is called local color. The dense fog of "Scandals of England" mentioned above is*

Is to express the local color of London. And in "Bringing Up Baby," the leopard, on the one hand, could express the power of the Queen, and on the other hand, it also*

Can express the local color of the Sahara. As for the famous film "The Golden Mountain," a woman eating sunflower seeds, this is even more indicative of the local color of the Caucasus*

The local color of the area.

If Chinese filmmakers want the audience to know the location where the story takes place, a slightly more sophisticated approach would be to use Sassoon House*

Etc. to represent Shanghai, the Temple of Heaven etc. to represent Beijing, and a more clumsy approach would be to simply use subtitles to explain. This has very little effect.*

Very little.

In any case, form is always determined by content, and the method of creation is the basis of all art. "The natural world is only a frame for people-" "The natural world is not dead, not indifferent at all"; "The natural world is sometimes like a pastoral poem filled with gentleness and affection, and sometimes as frightening as thunder and lightning"; "Nature - this is a force, a force that directly participates in major and minor events, an untiring witness, a good friend, or a vicious enemy." (G. Nela Tofu's preface to "The Iron Flood") So to use*

The natural world to express local color, we should also express the dynamics of the natural world. The dense fog of "Scandals of England" is very*

Appropriately matched with the sound of the milk cart bell to weave a "poetic haziness." Simply introducing the Temple of Heaven or Sassoon House in a stiff manner is not*

It's useless. What's more, the fog in "Scandals of England" is still related to the plot. In the fog, seeing a woman not very clearly caused*

Misunderstanding. The woman eating sunflower seeds in "The Golden Mountain," in addition to expressing the local color, also expresses their leisurely mood at the time*

State of mind, not to mention the leopard's display of power in "Bringing Up Baby."

As for the same "existence," becoming two completely different atmospheres due to different methods of expression, there are more examples to cite. The*

The smokestack screen of "The Golden Mountain," because the camera is close to the smokestack and more smoke is captured, makes the audience feel the greatness and horror of the factory. The*

The smokestack in the domestic film "Oppression," because the camera is far away, includes the factory roof and because it is meant to show that the factory is closed and there is no smoke, gives people the impression*

The feeling of a landscape painting, I think if this shot were closer, in the picture it was a close-up of the top half of the smokestack*,

I think the audience would not have the feeling of a landscape painting.

Artists, give nature and life peace, only in this way can we achieve the best effect of atmosphere and local color.

Film Reviews

Review of "Spring Love" The Song You Gave Me - Guotai I 259

— Ya Fu

Upon seeing the title "Spring Love," it reminded me of the cartoon "Spring Outing" in a recent "Free Talk" column, and I smiled.

Love, love, love through and through, romance through and through. It also carries a touch of melancholy. Perhaps, those dignified individuals who have been disappointed in love affairs will be moved by the Sentiment written with a light touch, but isn't this also a joke?

Because the playwright wanted to write a so-called lovely romance, he cleverly wrote this cinematic entanglement of men and women. Indeed, the film fully utilizes the expression techniques unique to cinema (such as Bipitada Nair pretending to kiss others behind the door), making this romance very vivid and interesting. Conversely, it could not be so fully expressed in literature. Technique is always determined by content, and romance has its own unique techniques.

Furthermore, each actor appropriately makes this romance struggle to exist. It is not only Bipitada Nair who has done her utmost; even the three supporting actors are directed in a very lively and interesting way. Therefore, from all aspects, this "Spring Love" is not in the center of Rofnanism films, but it occupies its place and is a new type, which is not commonly seen in British and American films. If someone is moved by it and then denies that it is romance, then we only need to consider the fact that the singer does not marry any of the people surrounding her, but instead unites with that rather impoverished opera performer – this is the playwright's greatest fantasy. However, here lies the origin of the playwright's sadness: he sympathizes with the plight of the famous singer, believing that in all the world, only the unestablished musician truly loves her and understands her.

Currently, a small number of people consider film to be a "soft art," a term used very strangely. It is explained that because the film is soft, the film can be without consciousness. Then I think this "Spring Love" should be most suitable for their taste.

Finally, I think the puppet show in the play is worth seeing. For the sake of theatrical research, we may wish to learn from it. As for what effect this kind of film will have on the audience in the current turbulent situation, I think it goes without saying.

Audience Opinions

Regarding "Sports Queen" 260

— Hu Yue

Some people who have seen "Sports Queen" think that its main point is to break the championship system in the sports world and criticize the golden crown of the sports queen, which is very good. First of all, this gentleman does not understand the reason for the existence of the championship system, which has profound social reasons. The commodification of education has turned sports competitions into trademarks for commodities, used to appeal to their patrons, so there must be a championship system to encourage a group of warriors. The various corrupt and degenerate phenomena of modern society, economic bankruptcy, and political darkness, are placed in front of the students, shaking the hearts of most of them. Those with clearer minds are naturally very dissatisfied with this situation, so these students are hated by people, and many methods are used to disrupt the students' vision. "Sports" is one of them, using the championship system to strengthen the stimulation of sports, making it easier to complete the current task of "sports." On the other hand, the championship system itself is beyond reproach, but because the championship system is used in the current education system, which is fundamentally anti-progressive, general superficial observers always believe that the championship system should be broken, but they forget the anti-progressive nature of the current sports education.

This gentleman does not know this, and he has not seen what the author of "Sports Queen" wanted to say but dared not say explicitly. When the world war broke out, the people of various countries were deceived by what was called "glory" and sacrificed in vain, just like Qiu Hua sacrificed in the sports arena. On the eve of World War II, we should realize that so-called "glory" has nothing to do with the people, and the people should no longer sacrifice in vain. In front of the people is struggle and progress!

[Ｉ> One scene from "Tiger Demon King," which will be shown in Shanghai soon <Ｉ]

Impressions After Seeing "The Fugitive" 261

— Li Tian

The impression that the film gives the audience is like a fleeting dream, disappearing like smoke, undoubtedly a failed production. Another kind of film not only engraves endless traces in the depths of your mind, but also further triggers your profound thinking. The "?" symbol constantly revolves in your brain; that is a successful blockbuster.

I don't like the so-called song and dance blockbusters that are full of carnal and fragrant scenes; I don't want to see the love story of talented scholars and beautiful ladies under the moonlight; I don't want to see wild beasts and natives being cruelly chased by civilized people. I eagerly hope that films with social significance will provide us with spiritual food.

"The Fugitive," in my mind, is a successful blockbuster and a film with social significance. It exposes the darkness and pain of prison life, the cruelty of the jailers, and the corruption of the prison system. We must know that this is a serious social problem!

Paul Muni is indeed a successful person in the film industry. His expression is not just on his face. In his whole body, there is a burning emotion of fierce resistance, a manifestation of the inner self.

Alan's two risky escapes are enough to make us hold our breath. The jailers' whipping of the prisoners reminds me of all the brutal systems in our country's prisons. Let's think about it, are prisons and laws the only way to bring prisoners back on the right track?

When Alan whispered to Helen, "I am leaving, and this life will end as a fugitive. Please don't think of me again!" Can one not be heartbroken as a fugitive? May I ask, who is to blame for the creation of fugitives?

The clanging of iron chains, the shouts in the mine, the sound of gunfire chasing, the barking of hunting dogs, and the whispers of farewell still echo in my mind. Paul Muni's profound performance and thought-provoking plot reappear before my eyes.

"Iron Bird" Only One Interior Scene Remaining 262

"Iron Bird," directed by Yuan Congmei, is the first aviation film in the history of Chinese cinema. Because this film received help from the Central Aviation School, it has gained unexpected achievements in the aviation part.

This play, after the efforts of Yuan Congmei and all the cast and crew, has completed nine-tenths of the entire drama. Now, only one interior scene remains. When this interior scene is filmed, the entire drama will be completed successfully.

It is said that the set for this scene is very grand, so it is necessary to increase the number of workers and it will also take some time to build. However, it is expected that it will be completed by the middle of this month.

Film Novel

Records of War Drums and Sword Shadows (Nana) (7) 263

— Yin Ming

Nana said frankly: "I have nothing to say. I don't think there is anything shameful about my love. To ask me to deny my love or apologize for my love is to blaspheme and despise it. Greina, no matter what you scold me, I can never blaspheme or despise my love." The old man shouted furiously: "See what you are without me. Get out! Get out!" Go to the street! Without Greina, don't even think about having a place to eat. You try!" Nana slowly walked to the door. When she reached the door, she turned back and said to Greina, "Thank you, Gejina, for everything you have done for me. I will always remember that my first meeting with the only person I love was in your theater." After she finished speaking, she quietly left.

Greina was not bad. He was a man of wealth and power. He used his money and power to make it impossible for Nana to find any work in all the theaters in Paris. At first, she sold some of the jewelry she had brought with her to make a living, living in a dilapidated small house, while her old friends, Mimi and Sanding, still relied on her. Not only Mimi and Sanding, but also Su Yi lived with her, because Greina determined that she must also be an accomplice and fired her. Returning to a life of poverty, Nana didn't care much. She treated this arrival of frustration just as she had treated the arrival of success not long ago, calmly and without surprise. After some time, she seemed to have forgotten the glory of the surging sound and applause in the theater. There was only one thing that made her feel uneasy day and night... That was that after George left, there was no news at all. She wrote many letters to him, but it was in vain. Now she was sitting at a broken desk again, writing a letter... She always hoped that this letter might get a reply. After she finished writing, she raised her head and said sadly to Mimi, "I really don't understand... Even if we had a quarrel..." Mimi took the letter and asked her, "Poor baby, don't try to understand it. I'll mail it for you." Nana gave her a sad smile and said, "Yes, Mimi, thank you."

As soon as Mimi took Nana's letter and walked out of the room, she was stopped by Su Yi. She asked, "Is it another letter to George?" Mimi said, "Yes. I feel like I've committed some crime, always destroying other people's letters, and I feel uneasy. And George's letter, did another one come today?" Su Yi said, "Yes, another one came today. I'm already ashamed. This is a very difficult thing, and I know it. But someday she will be grateful to us. This matter probably won't last long. She's about to give in. She'll be with someone else soon." Mimi said, "George doesn't have much money. How can he support her? So as long as she can understand in her heart and find such a person, take out some money to enable her to return to the stage, then Greina will have to watch and there's nothing he can do." They secretly discussed like this, thinking that by that time, they could all enjoy endless pleasure again. (To be continued)
